Here's a summary of what was done:\n\n## Summary\n\nCreated a full formalization for Sergey Kardash's 2011 P=NP attempt (Woeginger's list #76) at `proofs/attempts/sergey-kardash-2011-peqnp/`.\n\n**The attempt**: Kardash's \"pair cleaning\" method iteratively removes inconsistent variable assignments from overlapping clause groups in a k-CNF formula, claiming the result is non-empty iff satisfiable — giving O(n^12) for 3-SAT.\n\n**The error**: Pair cleaning is equivalent to **arc consistency (AC-3)** from constraint programming. Arc consistency is polynomial and necessary for satisfiability, but is **not sufficient** for k ≥ 3 — arc-consistent formulas can still be unsatisfiable. The fatal gap is in Lemma 1's inductive step, which unjustifiably treats local pairwise consistency as global satisfiability.\n\n**Files created**:\n- `ORIGINAL.md` + `ORIGINAL.pdf` — full paper 1\n- `refutation/lean/KardashRefutation.lean` + `refutation/rocq/KardashRefutation.v` — showing arc consistency ≠ satisfiability\n\nPR: https://github.com/konard/p-vs-np/pull/548\n\n---\n*This summary Adds full formalization for Sergey Kardash's 2011 P=NP attempt (Woeginger's list entry #76).\\n\\n### The Attempt\\n\\nKardash proposed a \\\"pair cleaning\\\" algorithm to solve k-satisfiability in polynomial time O(n^12) for 3-SAT (arXiv:1108.0408). The method:\\n\\n1. Groups clauses by their variable index sets into \\\"clause groups\\\"\\n2. Forms all C(nt, k+1) \\\"clause combinations\\\" (sets of k+1 overlapping groups)\\n3. Iteratively removes variable assignments from each combination's value table that have no compatible assignment in overlapping combinations\\n4. Claims the result is non-empty iff the formula is satisfiable\\n\\n### The Error\\n\\nThe pair cleaning method is exactly **arc consistency** (AC-3 in constraint programming). Arc consistency is:\\n- ✅ Polynomial to compute — the runtime claim O(n^12) is correct\\n- ✅ Necessary for satisfiability — empty result implies UNSAT\\n- ❌ NOT sufficient for satisfiability for k ≥ 3 — this is the error\\n\\n**The critical gap is in Lemma 1**: the inductive proof unjustifiably equates local pairwise consistency with global satisfiability. An arc-consistent k-SAT formula (k ≥ 3) can still be unsatisfiable. Classic example: a SAT encoding of a non-3-colorable graph passes all pairwise checks yet has no satisfying assignment.\\n\\nNote: Arc consistency IS complete for k=2 (Krom 1967), which is why 2-SAT ∈ P.\\n\\n### Files Added\\n\\n```\\nproofs/attempts/sergey-kardash-2011-peqnp/\\n├── ORIGINAL.md           # English markdown of arXiv:1108.0408\\n├── ORIGINAL.pdf          # Original paper PDF\\n├── README.md             # Description, error analysis, references\\n├── proof/\\n│   ├── README.md\\n│   ├── lean/KardashProof.lean    # Lean 4 formalization of claimed algorithm\\n│   └── rocq/KardashProof.v      # Rocq formalization of claimed algorithm\\n└── refutation/\\n    ├── README.md\\n    ├── lean/KardashRefutation.lean   # Lean 4 refutation (arc consistency incomplete)\\n    └── rocq/KardashRefutation.v      # Rocq refutation\\n```\\n\\n- `sorry` / `Admitted` marks the exact point where Kardash's proof fails (Theorem 1 / Lemma 1 inductive step)\\n- ATTEMPTS.md updated in alphabetical order\",\"comments\":[{\"id\":\"IC_kwDOQBQH6M8AAAABAK5QHA\",\"author\":{\"login\":\"konard\"},\"authorAssociation\":\"OWNER\",\"body\":\"## Solution summary\\n\\nThe implementation is complete. Here's a summary of what was done:\n\n## Summary\n\nCreated a full formalization for Sergey Kardash's 2011 P=NP attempt (Woeginger's list #76) at `proofs/attempts/sergey-kardash-2011-peqnp/`.\n\n**The attempt**: Kardash's \"pair cleaning\" method iteratively removes inconsistent variable assignments from overlapping clause groups in a k-CNF formula, claiming the result is non-empty iff satisfiable — giving O(n^12) for 3-SAT.\n\n**The error**: Pair cleaning is equivalent to **arc consistency (AC-3)** from constraint programming. Arc consistency is polynomial and necessary for satisfiability, but is **not sufficient** for k ≥ 3 — arc-consistent formulas can still be unsatisfiable. The fatal gap is in Lemma 1's inductive step, which unjustifiably treats local pairwise consistency as global satisfiability.\n\n**Files created**:\n- `ORIGINAL.md` + `ORIGINAL.pdf` — full paper (arXiv:1108.0408)\n- `README.md` — description and error analysis\n- `proof/lean/KardashProof.lean` + `proof/rocq/KardashProof.v` — formalizing the claimed algorithm with `sorry`/`Admitted` at Theorem 1\n- `refutation/lean/KardashRefutation.lean` + `refutation/rocq/KardashRefutation.v` — showing arc consistency ≠ satisfiability\n\nPR: https://github.com/konard/p-vs-np/pull/548\n\n---\n*This summary Here's a summary of what was done:\n\n## Summary\n\nCreated a full formalization for Sergey Kardash's 2011 P=NP attempt (Woeginger's list #76) at `proofs/attempts/sergey-kardash-2011-peqnp/`.\n\n**The attempt**: Kardash's \"pair cleaning\" method iteratively removes inconsistent variable assignments from overlapping clause groups in a k-CNF formula, claiming the result is non-empty iff satisfiable — giving O(n^12) for 3-SAT.\n\n**The error**: Pair cleaning is equivalent to **arc consistency (AC-3)** from constraint programming. Arc consistency is polynomial and necessary for satisfiability, but is **not sufficient** for k ≥ 3 — arc-consistent formulas can still be unsatisfiable. The fatal gap is in Lemma 1's inductive step, which unjustifiably treats local pairwise consistency as global satisfiability.\n\n**Files created**:\n- `ORIGINAL.md` + `ORIGINAL.pdf` — full paper (arXiv:1108.0408)\n- `README.md` — description and error analysis\n- `proof/lean/KardashProof.lean` + `proof/rocq/KardashProof.v` — formalizing the claimed algorithm with `sorry`/`Admitted` at Theorem 1\n- `refutation/lean/KardashRefutation.lean` + `refutation/rocq/KardashRefutation.v` — showing arc consistency ≠ satisfiability\n\nPR: https://github.com/konard/p-vs-np/pull/548\n\n---\n*This summary Here's a summary of what was done:\n\n## Summary\n\nCreated a full formalization for Sergey Kardash's 2011 P=NP attempt (Woeginger's list #76) at `proofs/attempts/sergey-kardash-2011-peqnp/`.\n\n**The attempt**: Kardash's \"pair cleaning\" method iteratively removes inconsistent variable assignments from overlapping clause groups in a k-CNF formula, claiming the result is non-empty iff satisfiable — giving O(n^12) for 3-SAT.\n\n**The error**: Pair cleaning is equivalent to **arc consistency (AC-3)** from constraint programming. Arc consistency is polynomial and necessary for satisfiability, but is **not sufficient** for k ≥ 3 — arc-consistent formulas can still be unsatisfiable. The fatal gap is in Lemma 1's inductive step, which unjustifiably treats local pairwise consistency as global satisfiability.\n\n**Files created**:\n- `ORIGINAL.md` + `ORIGINAL.pdf` — full paper 1\n- `refutation/lean/KardashRefutation.lean` + `refutation/rocq/KardashRefutation.v` — showing arc consistency ≠ satisfiability\n\nPR: https://github.com/konard/p-vs-np/pull/548\n\n---\n*This summary Here's a summary of what was done:\n\n## Summary\n\nCreated a full formalization for Sergey Kardash's 2011 P=NP attempt (Woeginger's list #76) at `proofs/attempts/sergey-kardash-2011-peqnp/`.\n\n**The attempt**: Kardash's \"pair cleaning\" method iteratively removes inconsistent variable assignments from overlapping clause groups in a k-CNF formula, claiming the result is non-empty iff satisfiable — giving O(n^12) for 3-SAT.\n\n**The error**: Pair cleaning is equivalent to **arc consistency (AC-3)** from constraint programming. Arc consistency is polynomial and necessary for satisfiability, but is **not sufficient** for k ≥ 3 — arc-consistent formulas can still be unsatisfiable. The fatal gap is in Lemma 1's inductive step, which unjustifiably treats local pairwise consistency as global satisfiability.\n\n**Files created**:\n- `ORIGINAL.md` + `ORIGINAL.pdf` — full paper 1\n- `refutation/lean/KardashRefutation.lean` + `refutation/rocq/KardashRefutation.v` — showing arc consistency ≠ satisfiability\n\nPR: https://github.com/konard/p-vs-np/pull/548\n\n---\n*This summary Here's a summary of what was done:\n\n## Summary\n\nCreated a full formalization for Sergey Kardash's 2011 P=NP attempt (Woeginger's list #76) at `proofs/attempts/sergey-kardash-2011-peqnp/`.\n\n**The attempt**: Kardash's \"pair cleaning\" method iteratively removes inconsistent variable assignments from overlapping clause groups in a k-CNF formula, claiming the result is non-empty iff satisfiable — giving O(n^12) for 3-SAT.\n\n**The error**: Pair cleaning is equivalent to **arc consistency (AC-3)** from constraint programming. Arc consistency is polynomial and necessary for satisfiability, but is **not sufficient** for k ≥ 3 — arc-consistent formulas can still be unsatisfiable. The fatal gap is in Lemma 1's inductive step, which unjustifiably treats local pairwise consistency as global satisfiability.\n\n**Files created**:\n- `ORIGINAL.md` + `ORIGINAL.pdf` — full paper (arXiv:1108.0408)\n- `README.md` — description and error analysis\n- `proof/lean/KardashProof.lean` + `proof/rocq/KardashProof.v` — formalizing the claimed algorithm with `sorry`/`Admitted` at Theorem 1\n- `refutation/lean/KardashRefutation.lean` + `refutation/rocq/KardashRefutation.v` — showing arc consistency ≠ satisfiability\n\nPR: https://github.com/konard/p-vs-np/pull/548\n\n---\n*This summary Here's a summary of what was done:\n\n## Summary\n\nCreated a full formalization for Sergey Kardash's 2011 P=NP attempt (Woeginger's list #76) at `proofs/attempts/sergey-kardash-2011-peqnp/`.\n\n**The attempt**: Kardash's \"pair cleaning\" method iteratively removes inconsistent variable assignments from overlapping clause groups in a k-CNF formula, claiming the result is non-empty iff satisfiable — giving O(n^12) for 3-SAT.\n\n**The error**: Pair cleaning is equivalent to **arc consistency (AC-3)** from constraint programming. Arc consistency is polynomial and necessary for satisfiability, but is **not sufficient** for k ≥ 3 — arc-consistent formulas can still be unsatisfiable. The fatal gap is in Lemma 1's inductive step, which unjustifiably treats local pairwise consistency as global satisfiability.\n\n**Files created**:\n- `ORIGINAL.md` + `ORIGINAL.pdf` — full paper (arXiv:1108.0408)\n- `README.md` — description and error analysis\n- `proof/lean/KardashProof.lean` + `proof/rocq/KardashProof.v` — formalizing the claimed algorithm with `sorry`/`Admitted` at Theorem 1\n- `refutation/lean/KardashRefutation.lean` + `refutation/rocq/KardashRefutation.v` — showing arc consistency ≠ satisfiability\n\nPR: https://github.com/konard/p-vs-np/pull/548\n\n---\n*This summary Here's a summary of what was done:\n\n## Summary\n\nCreated a full formalization for Sergey Kardash's 2011 P=NP attempt (Woeginger's list #76) at `proofs/attempts/sergey-kardash-2011-peqnp/`.\n\n**The attempt**: Kardash's \"pair cleaning\" method iteratively removes inconsistent variable assignments from overlapping clause groups in a k-CNF formula, claiming the result is non-empty iff satisfiable — giving O(n^12) for 3-SAT.\n\n**The error**: Pair cleaning is equivalent to **arc consistency (AC-3)** from constraint programming. Arc consistency is polynomial and necessary for satisfiability, but is **not sufficient** for k ≥ 3 — arc-consistent formulas can still be unsatisfiable. The fatal gap is in Lemma 1's inductive step, which unjustifiably treats local pairwise consistency as global satisfiability.\n\n**Files created**:\n- `ORIGINAL.md` + `ORIGINAL.pdf` — full paper 1\n- `refutation/lean/KardashRefutation.lean` + `refutation/rocq/KardashRefutation.v` — showing arc consistency ≠ satisfiability\n\nPR: https://github.com/konard/p-vs-np/pull/548\n\n---\n*This summary Here's a summary of what was done:\n\n## Summary\n\nCreated a full formalization for Sergey Kardash's 2011 P=NP attempt (Woeginger's list #76) at `proofs/attempts/sergey-kardash-2011-peqnp/`.\n\n**The attempt**: Kardash's \"pair cleaning\" method iteratively removes inconsistent variable assignments from overlapping clause groups in a k-CNF formula, claiming the result is non-empty iff satisfiable — giving O(n^12) for 3-SAT.\n\n**The error**: Pair cleaning is equivalent to **arc consistency (AC-3)** from constraint programming. Arc consistency is polynomial and necessary for satisfiability, but is **not sufficient** for k ≥ 3 — arc-consistent formulas can still be unsatisfiable. The fatal gap is in Lemma 1's inductive step, which unjustifiably treats local pairwise consistency as global satisfiability.\n\n**Files created**:\n- `ORIGINAL.md` + `ORIGINAL.pdf` — full paper (arXiv:1108.0408)\n- `README.md` — description and error analysis\n- `proof/lean/KardashProof.lean` + `proof/rocq/KardashProof.v` — formalizing the claimed algorithm with `sorry`/`Admitted` at Theorem 1\n- `refutation/lean/KardashRefutation.lean` + `refutation/rocq/KardashRefutation.v` — showing arc consistency ≠ satisfiability\n\nPR: https://github.com/konard/p-vs-np/pull/548\n\n---\n*This summary Here's a summary of what was done:\n\n## Summary\n\nCreated a full formalization for Sergey Kardash's 2011 P=NP attempt (Woeginger's list #76) at `proofs/attempts/sergey-kardash-2011-peqnp/`.\n\n**The attempt**: Kardash's \"pair cleaning\" method iteratively removes inconsistent variable assignments from overlapping clause groups in a k-CNF formula, claiming the result is non-empty iff satisfiable — giving O(n^12) for 3-SAT.\n\n**The error**: Pair cleaning is equivalent to **arc consistency (AC-3)** from constraint programming. Arc consistency is polynomial and necessary for satisfiability, but is **not sufficient** for k ≥ 3 — arc-consistent formulas can still be unsatisfiable. The fatal gap is in Lemma 1's inductive step, which unjustifiably treats local pairwise consistency as global satisfiability.\n\n**Files created**:\n- `ORIGINAL.md` + `ORIGINAL.pdf` — full paper 1\n- `refutation/lean/KardashRefutation.lean` + `refutation/rocq/KardashRefutation.v` — showing arc consistency ≠ satisfiability\n\nPR: https://github.com/konard/p-vs-np/pull/548\n\n---\n*This summary
